Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by October 14, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

The notice explains why we transferred your case. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your notice by October 29, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
